    SELECT [u].[UserId], [u].[AvatarUrl], [u].[CreatedAt], [u].[Email], [u].[FullName], [u].[IsActive], [u].[IsEmailVerified], [u].[LastLoginAt], [u].[PasswordHash], [u].[PhoneNumber], [u].[RoleId], [u].[SchoolId], [u].[UpdatedAt], [r].[RoleId] AS [RoleId0], [r].[Description], [r].[RoleCode], [r].[RoleName]
    FROM [Users] AS [u]
    INNER JOIN [Roles] AS [r] ON [u].[RoleId] = [r].[RoleId]
    WHERE [u].[SchoolId] = @__schoolId_0 AND [r].[RoleCode] IN (N'STUDENT', N'TEACHER', N'SUPERVISOR', N'PARENT')
    ORDER BY [u].[CreatedAt] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_1 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_2 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [StudentProfiles] AS [s] ON [t].[UserId] = [s].[UserId]
LEFT JOIN [TeacherProfiles] AS [t0] ON [t].[UserId] = [t0].[UserId]
LEFT JOIN [Subjects] AS [s0] ON [t0].[PrimarySubjectId] = [s0].[SubjectId]
LEFT JOIN [SupervisorProfiles] AS [s1] ON [t].[UserId] = [s1].[UserId]
LEFT JOIN [ParentProfiles] AS [p] ON [t].[UserId] = [p].[UserId]
ORDER BY [t].[CreatedAt] DESC
